However, multiple reviewers noted that the phrasing '   ' feels awkward, somewhat literal, and less natural in contemporary Uyghur. Suggested improvements include replacing '' with more fluid terms like ' ' (visited), '' (approached), or ' ' (visited), and simplifying or modernizing the phrase to enhance readability and flow. 5. Preserve clarity and naturalness: The translation should remain clear and accessible without awkwardness, promoting reader engagement and understanding.
